<div id="terms_and_conditions">
 <h2 class="ally-header--standard-heavy">
  Important Fare &amp; Schedule Information
 </h2>
 <ul>
  <li>
   All fares and fare ranges are subject to change until purchased.
  </li>
  <li>
   Flight ontime performance statistics can be viewed by clicking on the individual flight numbers.
  </li>
  <li>
   All fares and fare ranges listed are per person for each way of travel.
  </li>
  <li>
   <span class="bugRedText">
    “Unavailable”
   </span>
   indicates the corresponding fare is unavailable for the selected travel date(s), the search did not meet certain fare requirements, or the flight has already departed.
  </li>
  <li>
   <span class="bugRedText">
    “Sold Out”
   </span>
   indicates that the flight is sold out for the corresponding fare type or the number of passengers in your reservation exceeds the number of remaining available seats for the corresponding fare type.
  </li>
  <li>
   <span class="bugRedText">
    “Invalid w/ Depart or Return Dates”
   </span>
   indicates that our system cannot return a valid itinerary option(s) with the search criteria submitted. This can occur when flights are sold out in one direction of a roundtrip search or with a same-day roundtrip search. These itineraries may become valid options if you search with a different depart or return date and/or for a one way flight instead.
  </li>
  <li class="multiPaxAdultOnly">
   “Available” in the Senior Fare column indicates the Senior Fare is available for the flight and may be selected for the Senior Passenger, after selecting a fare for the Adult Passenger on this page.
  </li>
  <li>
   “Travel Time” represents the total elapsed time for your trip from your departure city to your final destination including stops, layovers, and time zone changes.
  </li>
  <li class="a11y-wrapper">
   Along with our everyday low fares you may inquire about our discounts off the “Anytime” fare for
   <a aria-describedby="a11y-message--new-window" class="a11y-link a11y-link--underline" href="/html/customer-service/family/baby-on-board-pol.html" target="_blank">
    infant
   </a>
   ,
   <a aria-describedby="a11y-message--new-window" class="a11y-link a11y-link--underline" href="/html/customer-service/family/children-pol.html" target="_blank">
    child (2-11)
   </a>
   , and
   <a aria-describedby="a11y-message--new-window" class="a11y-link a11y-link--underline" href="/html/customer-service/how-tos/book-and-manage-air-pol.html" target="_blank">
    military
   </a>
   fares by calling 1-800-I-FLY-SWA (1-800-435-9792).
  </li>
  <li class="a11y-wrapper">
   <a aria-describedby="a11y-message--new-window" class="a11y-link a11y-link--underline" href="/html/air/business-groups/group-travel.html" target="_blank">
    Group Reservations:
   </a>
   Ten or more Customers traveling from/to the same origin/destination. Discounts vary. Call 1-800-433-5368.
  </li>
  <!--mp_trans_add
    <li>All prices displayed on this web page are in dollars of the United States of America.</li> -->
 </ul>
 <ul>
  <li class="a11y-wrapper">
   *Savings based on Southwest Vacations Flight + Hotel package bookings of 5 or more nights on
   <a aria-describedby="a11y-message--new-window" class="a11y-link a11y-link--underline" href="http://www.southwestvacations.com" target="_blank">
    www.southwestvacations.com
   </a>
   from June 1, 2015 through October 31, 2015, as compared to the price of the same components booked separately on southwest.com. Savings on any given package will vary based on the selected origin, destination, travel dates, number of passengers, hotel property, length of stay, car rental, and activity tickets. Savings may not be available on all packages.
  </li>
 </ul>
</div>

       <span>
        <strong>
         No Show Policy:
        </strong>
        If you are not planning to travel on any portion of this itinerary, please cancel your reservation at least 10 minutes prior to scheduled departure of the flight. Customers who fail to cancel or change a Wanna Get Away segment at least 10 minutes prior to travel and who do not board the flight, will be considered a no show, and all remaining funds on this reservation will be forfeited, including Business Select and Anytime funds. On cancellations, 100% of the ticket value may be applied to future travel to be completed for up to 12 months or by your ticket's expiration date, whichever comes first.
        <br>
         <strong>
          Canceling your reservations without penalty:
         </strong>
         If you call or cancel online at
         <b>
          Southwest.com
         </b>
         within 24 hours of booking, Southwest will offer you the option of refunding the airfare back to the original form of payment, or retaining the credit to be used toward future travel.
        </br>
       </span>

        <sup>
         ®
        </sup>
        coffee onboard all flights. Baggage weight and size limits apply.
       </span>

 <script type="text/cjs">
  $("#pointsLoginModalButton").click(function() {
            return validateLoyaltyLogin();
        });


        function validateLoyaltyLogin(formSubmissionError) {

            var $errorsWrapper = $(".points-login-modal--errors-wrapper");
            var $loginFieldWithError = $(".points-login-modal .fieldError");
            var $loginField = $(".points-login-modal .modalInput");

            $errorsWrapper.html("");
            $loginFieldWithError.removeClass("fieldError").removeAttr('aria-invalid');

            $loginField.filter(function (o) { return $(this).attr("value") == "" }).addClass("fieldError");

            var hasErrors = $loginField.hasClass("fieldError");

            if(formSubmissionError != undefined || hasErrors) {
                if(formSubmissionError != undefined) {
                    $errorsWrapper.html(swa.errors.messages[formSubmissionError]);
                } else {
                    var errorBullets = "";
                    $loginFieldWithError = $(".points-login-modal .fieldError");
                    $loginFieldWithError.each(function() {
                        var id = $(this).attr("data");
                        errorBullets = errorBullets + "<div>" + swa.errors.messages[id] + "</div>";
                    });
                    $errorsWrapper.html(errorBullets);
                }
                accountNavLoginErrors($loginField, $errorsWrapper);
            }

            if (hasErrors === false) {
                return true;
            } else {
                return false;
            }
        }

        if(swa.loginModalValidationError != undefined) {
            openPointsLoginModal();
            validateLoyaltyLogin(swa.loginModalValidationError);
        }

        function openPointsLoginModal() {
            var $loginModal = $('#pointsLoginModal');
            var $triggerElement = $('.skip-top-navigation--link');

            $loginModal.modal();
            $loginModal.parents('#simplemodal-container').addClass('simplemodal-container-no-bg');
            new popUpAccessible($loginModal, $triggerElement, $.modal.close, '.simplemodal-close', true);

            return false;
        }
 </script>
</div>

 <script type="text/javascript">
  (typeof bindPointsInPathModal === "function") ? bindPointsInPathModal('.js-ad-buy-points-link') : '';
    var isEnough = false;
    var fareTypeOptions = {"Dollars": 'dollars', "Points": 'points'};
    var fareType = $('button.js-base-button-points').length ? fareTypeOptions.Points : fareTypeOptions.Dollars;
    var isLoggedIn = $('form .logoutLink').length ? true : false;
    var isBannerDisplayed = $('#not-enough-points-link').length ? true : false;
    var isMember = false;

    if (fareType === 'points' && !isBannerDisplayed) {
        isEnough = true;
    }

    if (fareType === 'points' && isLoggedIn === true && swa.loggedInUserType === 'member') {
        isMember = true;
    }

    mboxDefine('tagcontainer_points_ad','swa_select_flight_pip_image','fareType='+fareType,'auth='+isLoggedIn,'enough='+isEnough,'member='+isMember);
    mboxUpdate('swa_select_flight_pip_image','fareType='+fareType,'auth='+isLoggedIn,'enough='+isEnough,'member='+isMember);
 </script>

            };
